"AllVehiclesDevScene-wEntry" Scene Setup Steps
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Description:

Create a basic All Vehicle Controller(s) with entry in scene for your Unity
projects using vehicle models from Synty Polygon Heist Asset.


Player Controls:
----------------

Player Forward:   W
Player Reverse:   S
Player Left:      A
Player Right:     D
Player Jump:      Space
Player Sprint:    Left Shift


Vehicle Controls: 
-----------------

Vehicle Forward:  W
Vehicle Reverse:  S
Turn Left:        A
Turn Right:       D
Apply Brake:      Space
Enter Vehicle:    E
Exit Vehicle:     F


Helicopter Controls: 
--------------------

Heli Roll:        A & D
Heli Pitch:       S & W
Heli Yaw:         Q & E
Enter Vehicle:    E
Exit Vehicle:     F

Decrease throttle: Left Shift
Increase throttle: Left Control


Helicopter Camera Controls:
---------------------------

Change Cameras: V (ie: Rear Camera, Belly Camera & Cockpit Camera)


Manual Setup Instruction:
-------------------------

* Simply follow the instruction for manual setup found below.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Prep Step: Create New Scene Called: "AllVehiclesDevScene-wEntry"

Note: if you already have some sort of a test terrain in place, well then, you
can simple skip the steps: #1, 2 & 3 and go directly to #4.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 1: Create: "Environment" * (for Nicer Organization)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create Empty: "Environment"

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

First since this is just a "holder" added for better organization, let us go
ahead & drag the "Directional Light" into "Environment".

* also if you wanted you could add a "dir" called Environment and opt to place
  your TerrainData inside that in its own Dir "TerrainData" and as such any
  other Environment stuff respectively in as desired the "Environment" dir.
  Just a suggestion.

Also: We don't need the "Main Camera" in Sample Scene, so..., we can go ahead
and delete it.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 2: Create: "Terrain Plane"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create New 3D Object: "Plane"

Position: X: 0   Y: -0.03 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0   Y: 0     Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 800 Y: 1     Z: 800

Rename to: "Terrain Plane"

We can now opt to clean up for better organization, simply drag the:
"Terrain Plane" into the holder "Environment" we added for just this exact
 purpose!


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 3: Create: "Terrain"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create New 3D Object: "Terrain"

Modify via:

"Terrain" Inspector: Terrain Settings

Mesh Resolution:

Terrain Width: 8000
Terrain Length: 8000

Modify via:

"Terrain" Inspector: "Transform"

Position: X: -4000 Y: 0 Z: -4000 
Rotation: X: 0     Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1     Y: 1 Z: 1

We can now opt to clean up for better organization, simply drag the:
"Terrain" into the holder "Environment" we added for just this exact purpose!


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 4: Create: empty "Vehicles"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create Empty: "Vehicles"

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Notes: Current Summary

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: Ok, by now your scene heirarchy at top should look like this:

Environment
Vehicle


Nice and organized right?! :) Good Stuff! ;)

Note: as this uses a vehicle from such and due to licensing such vehicles
cannot be included in this repository obviously, as such the provided scripts
and instructions thus require having / purchasing the:

Synty Polygon Heist Asset:

https://assetstore.unity.com/packages/3d/environments/urban/polygon-heist-low-poly-3d-art-by-synty-97949


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 5: Install: "Synty Polygon Heist Asset"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Depending on how you purchased you can either use the package manager to
install the asset or if you are like me and say already have local repository
storage of purchased assets and have the package already you can install the
asset manually.

Asset package to install:

 POLYGON Heist - Low Poly 3D Art by Synty.unitypackage

Purchase Synty Polygon Heist Asset:

https://assetstore.unity.com/packages/3d/environments/urban/polygon-heist-low-poly-3d-art-by-synty-97949


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 6: Identify: the "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonHeist > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 7: Add: the "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_01 => "PoliceCharger01"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: -9 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonHeist_Material_01_A

Then move "PoliceCharger01" into the empty: "Vehicles" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 8: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger01" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 9: Add: "Camera" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "PoliceCharger01Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "PoliceCharger01Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 1.64 Z: -6.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 10: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger01" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

Set the Transform of "WheelMeshes":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Copy & paste the following meshes into "WheelMeshes" as children
(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr

Transforms should be fine and unaffected but, let us just mention them for
good measure.

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7880916 Y: 0.4267825 Z: 1.564265
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Important: Disable the Sphere Collider Component!

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7992286 Y: 0.4267825 Z: 1.564265 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Important: Disable the Sphere Collider Component!

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7880916 Y: 0.4267825 Z: -1.460021
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Important: Disable the Sphere Collider Component!

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7992286 Y: 0.4267825 Z: -1.460021
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Important: Disable the Sphere Collider Component!


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 11: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger01" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Front Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Front Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Front Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Rear Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Rear Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825

Set Front Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Front Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Rear Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Reart Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7880916 Y: 0.5767825 Z: 1.564265
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7992286 Y: 0.5767825 Z: 1.564265
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7880916 Y: 0.5767825 Z: -1.460021
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7992286 Y: 0.5767825 Z: -1.460021
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Notes: Current Summary

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: Ok, by now your vehicle heirarchy should look like this:

Mostly Collapsed:

Vehicles

    SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Glass
    SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Plates
    SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_SteeringW 
    WheelMeshes
    WheelColliders   
    View

Fully Expanded:

Vehicles

    SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Plates
    SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_SteeringW

      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr

      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
      SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr   
    View
      PoliceCharger01Camera


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 12: Add to: PoliceCharger01 (PoliceCharger01Controller.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (PoliceCharger01Controller.cs) to "PoliceCharger01"

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: PoliceCharger01 (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl (Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

Rigidbody Mass:
---------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 2500


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 13: Add to: PoliceCharger01Camera (PoliceCharger01Camera.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (PoliceCharger01Camera.cs) to "PoliceCharger01Camera"


Adjust Settings:

Transforms:
-----------

Police Cruiser: PoliceCharger01 (Transform)

Height: 3.28


You can keep settings as is or tweak them to your likings! *

* ie: (tweak camera height)

Height: 3.16


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 14: Create: empty "Interface"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create an empty called: "Interface"

Layer: "UI"

Transform: 
----------

Position: X: 0 Y: 0   Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0   Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1   Z: 1 


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 15: In "Interface" Add UI: "Canvas"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create as a child of "Interface" Add a UI: "Canvas"


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 16: Create as child of "Canvas" add empty: "VehiclesEntry"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create as a child of "Interface" add empty: "VehiclesEntry"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Bottom Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: 50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 17:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "PoliceCharger01_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "PoliceCharger01_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]

Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...

Step 18: Create: object "Player":

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create empty object and name such: "Player"

Transform: 
----------

Position: X: 0 Y: 0.9799998 Z: -15
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0  Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1  Z: 1

Add Tag: "Player"


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 19: Add: empty object "View":

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "Player" object, create a child of the "Player" object and name
such: "View"

Transform Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 20: Add: "Camera":

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In "Player" object, add a Camera component as child of "View" and name
such: "Camera"

Transform: 
----------

Position: X: 0 Y: 0.6 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0   Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1   Z: 1

Depth: "1" 

Add Tag: "MainCamera"


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 21: Edit: the "CharacterController" component:

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "Player" object, edit the "CharacterController" component:

Height: "1.8"


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 22: Add Component: "First Person Controller (Script)"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Add: "FirstPersonController.cs" script to object: "Player"


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 23: Setup: Audio Source and Footstep Sounds Audio Clips:

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In "Player" object edit: the "First Person Controller (Script)"

Footstep Source: Player (AudioSource)

Footstep Sounds: "4"

Element 0: "Footstep01"
Element 1: "Footstep02"
Element 2: "Footstep03"
Element 3: "Footstep04"

Step 24: Add to: PoliceCharger01 (PoliceCharger01Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (PoliceCharger01Entry.cs) to "PoliceCharger01"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

PoliceCharger01: PoliceCharger01
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: PoliceCharger01_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to your
  likings and needs:

Center: X: 0.07936704 Y: 0.8205938 Z: 0.4637029
Size: X: 4.241376 Y: 1.228981 Z: 1.03095


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 25: In Interface > Canvas create empty child: "VehiclesSpeed"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "VehiclesSpeed"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Bottom Left

Width: 300
Height: 300


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 26: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "PoliceCharger01Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger01Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text output display thus such would make sense to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 27: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add UI IMG: "PoliceCharger01_SpeedoGuage"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "PoliceCharger01_SpeedoGuage"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300


In: "Image"


Source Image: Speedometer-Guage

Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF


Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "PoliceCharger01_SpeedText"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 200
Height: 50

Text Input:
-----------

0 mph


Font Size: 36 *

Vertex Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF

Alignment: Center Middle

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.


Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 30: In Vehicles > PoliceCharger01 attach script: (PoliceCharger01Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach PoliceCharger01Speedometer script: (PoliceCharger01Speedometer.cs) to
Vehicle: "PoliceCharger01"

In: "PoliceCharger01" > PoliceCharger01 Speedometer (Script)

Adjust the minimal settings as far as what is min needed: (Needle IMG and
Speed Text)

Needle: PoliceCharger01_Needle

Speed Text: PoliceCharger01_SpeedText (Text Mesh Pro UGUI)

GameObjects:

Interface Parent Object: PoliceCharger01Speedometer
Interface IMG01 Object: PoliceCharger01_SpeedoGuage
Interface IMG02 Object: PoliceCharger01_SpeedoNeedle
Interface Text Object: PoliceCharger01_SpeedText


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: Lastly, in case you missed this notice previously, we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
this object in the editor.

Game Objects:

PoliceCharger01Speedometer
PoliceCharger01_SpeedoGuage
PoliceCharger01_SpeedoNeedle
PoliceCharger01_SpeedText

Step 36: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger02" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Front Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Front Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Front Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Rear Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Rear Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825

Set Front Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Front Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Rear Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Reart Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08

We will need to now edit these infos:

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text output display thus such would make sense to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.

Step 51: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger03" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Front Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Front Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Front Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Rear Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Rear Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825

Set Front Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Front Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Rear Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Reart Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08

We will need to now edit these infos:

---------------

Height: 100

Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Step 56: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "PoliceCharger03Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger03Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text output display thus such would make sense to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.

Step 62: Add: the next "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_01 => "PoliceCharger04"

Position: X: 9 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Step 70: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceCharger04" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Front Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Front Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Front Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Front Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Left Wheel Center X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Rear Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

Rear Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.4267825
Rear Right Wheel Center X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08 
Rear Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.5767825 (0.4267825+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation

In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.4267825

Set Front Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Front Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Rear Left "Wheel Collider" Center: X: 5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08
Set Reart Right "Wheel Collider" Center: X: -5.960464e-08 Y: 1.490116e-08  Z: 2.980232e-08

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.7880916 Y: 0.5767825 Z: 1.564265
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.7992286 Y: 0.5767825 Z: 1.564265

Step 71: Add to: PoliceCharger04 (PoliceCharger04Controller.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (PoliceCharger04Controller.cs) to "PoliceCharger04"

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: PoliceCharger04 (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl (Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_Car_Police_Heist_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

Rigidbody Mass:
---------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 2500

Step 72: Add to: PoliceCharger04Camera (PoliceCharger04Camera.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (PoliceCharger04Camera.cs) to "PoliceCharger04Camera"


Adjust Settings:

Transforms:
-----------

Police Cruiser: PoliceCharger04 (Transform)

Height: 3.28


You can keep settings as is or tweak them to your likings! *

* ie: (tweak camera height)

Height: 3.16

Step 73:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "PoliceCharger04_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "PoliceCharger04_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]

Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text output display thus such would make sense to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.

Step 80: Add Input: "Heli Roll"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In Edit -> Project Settings -> Input Manager:

Add Input Axes: "Heli Roll"

Name: Roll
Negative Button: left
Positive Button: right
Alt Negative Button: a
Alt Positive Button: d
Gravity: 3
Dead: 0.001
Sensitivity: 3
Snap: True (checked)
Invert: False (unchecked)
Type: Key or Mouse Button
Axis: X axis
Joy Num: Get Motion from all Joysticks

Note: this is using the old input system and while yes, you could modify the script
for new input system usage, currently that is not covered in the scope of this 
setup at this time.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 89: Modify Settings for: "PoliceHelicopter01Controller (Script)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: While the script will work fine and fill most of these settings by itself on 
Awake() as intended say as long as you say set the bare minimum for example rotor 
sound & transforms, hmm, let us just for good measure set all up in inspector 
instead. So, in saying such, your settings should simply look like such:

Script: PoliceHelicopter01Controller

Inputs:
-------

Heli Roll Input: Heli Roll
Heli Pitch Input: Heli Pitch
Heli Yaw Input: Heli Yaw
Min Throttle Key: Left Shift
Max Throttle Key: Left Control

Components:
-----------

Rigidbody: PoliceHelicopter01 (Rigidbody)
Mesh Collider: PoliceHelicopter01 (Mesh Collider)

Rb Adjustments:
---------------

Rigibody Mass: 360
Center Of Mass Offset: X: 0 Y: 0.7 Z: 1

Transforms:
-----------

Rotors Transform Top: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Main_01 (Transform)
Rotors Transform Tail: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Back_01 (Transform)

Amounts:
--------

Sensitivity: 500
Throttle Amount: 25
Max Thrust: 5
Rotor speed Modifier: 10

Airspeed:
---------

Airspeed Type: Mph *

* or Kmh depending on your desired choice

Max Airspeed: 160 *

* 160 is max suggested for Mph else say 260 for Kmh for example if such was
  selected

HUD:
----

Heli HUD: PoliceHelicopter01_HUD * 

* This will need to be returned to and to then be selected
once you set the interface text mesh pro hud item up in the later step as
described.

Audio:
------

Audio Source: PoliceHelicopter01 (Audio Source)
Rotor Sound: Helicopter01_Rotor

  be overwritten on awake

Step 100: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonHeist > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Helicopter_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 101: Add: the next "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Helicopter_01 => "PoliceHelicopter02"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: 36 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonHeist_Material_02_A

Then move "PoliceHelicopter02" into the empty: "Vehicle" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 102: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceHelicopter02" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 103: Add: "Camera(s)" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "Heli02 Cockpit Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "Heli02 Cockpit Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 2.058 Z: 2.33 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

* Disable the bool in Inspector as this camera is currently just added as an 
optional example and is not currently used, but you could opt for either or a 
future switch method or what not, hence why such is added as an example of three 
diff views.

In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "Heli02 Belly Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "Heli02 Belly Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0.3 Z: 2 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

* Disable the bool in Inspector as this camera is currently just added as an 
optional example and is not currently used, but you could opt for either or a 
future switch method or what not, hence why such is added as an example of three 
diff views.

In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "Heli02 Rear Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "Heli02 Rear Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 3.2 Z: -10.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

* Keep this camera Active as this is the camera we will use (for now).

Step 106: Modify Settings for: "PoliceHelicopter02Controller (Script)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: While the script will work fine and fill most of these settings by itself on 
Awake() as intended say as long as you say set the bare minimum for example rotor 
sound & transforms, hmm, let us just for good measure set all up in inspector 
instead. So, in saying such, your settings should simply look like such:

Script: PoliceHelicopter02Controller

Inputs:
-------

Heli Roll Input: Heli Roll
Heli Pitch Input: Heli Pitch
Heli Yaw Input: Heli Yaw
Min Throttle Key: Left Shift
Max Throttle Key: Left Control

Components:
-----------

Rigidbody: PoliceHelicopter02 (Rigidbody)
Mesh Collider: PoliceHelicopter02 (Mesh Collider)

Rb Adjustments:
---------------

Rigibody Mass: 360
Center Of Mass Offset: X: 0 Y: 0.7 Z: 1

Transforms:
-----------

Rotors Transform Top: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Main_01 (Transform)
Rotors Transform Tail: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Back_01 (Transform)

Amounts:
--------

Sensitivity: 500
Throttle Amount: 25
Max Thrust: 5
Rotor speed Modifier: 10

Airspeed:
---------

Airspeed Type: Mph *

* or Kmh depending on your desired choice

Max Airspeed: 160 *

* 160 is max suggested for Mph else say 260 for Kmh for example if such was
  selected

HUD:
----

Heli HUD: PoliceHelicopter02_HUD * 

* This will need to be returned to and to then be selected
once you set the interface text mesh pro hud item up in the later step as
described.

Audio:
------

Audio Source: PoliceHelicopter02 (Audio Source)
Rotor Sound: Helicopter02_Rotor


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 107: Modify Settings for: "Rigidbody (Component)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: While the script will work fine and fill these particular settings by itself 
on Awake() as intended hmm, let us just for good measure set such up in inspector 
instead. So, in saying such, your specific settings should simply look like such:

Mass: 360


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 108: Modify Settings for: "Mesh Collider (Component)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: While the script will work fine and fill this particular setting by itself

---------------

-----------

* Say if you selected speed type Kmh then such:

Throttle: 0 %
Airspeed: 0 kmh
Altitude: 0 m

* Say if you selected speed type Mph then such:

Throttle: 0 %
Airspeed: 0 mph
Altitude: 0 ft

* Note: that either or of the above can be added as placeholder as such will
  be overwritten on awake

Alignment: Left & Middle

Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

optional example and is not currently used, but you could opt for either or a 
future switch method or what not, hence why such is added as an example of three 
diff views.

Depth: 0

Position: X: 0 Y: 0.3 Z: 2 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

* Disable the bool in Inspector as this camera is currently just added as an 
optional example and is not currently used, but you could opt for either or a 
future switch method or what not, hence why such is added as an example of three 
diff views.

Depth: 0

Position: X: 0 Y: 3.2 Z: -10.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0

Step 121: Modify Settings for: "PoliceHelicopter03Controller (Script)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: While the script will work fine and fill most of these settings by itself on 
Awake() as intended say as long as you say set the bare minimum for example rotor 
sound & transforms, hmm, let us just for good measure set all up in inspector 
instead. So, in saying such, your settings should simply look like such:

Script: PoliceHelicopter03Controller

Inputs:
-------

Heli Roll Input: Heli Roll
Heli Pitch Input: Heli Pitch
Heli Yaw Input: Heli Yaw
Min Throttle Key: Left Shift
Max Throttle Key: Left Control

Components:
-----------

Rigidbody: PoliceHelicopter03 (Rigidbody)
Mesh Collider: PoliceHelicopter03 (Mesh Collider)

Rb Adjustments:
---------------

Rigibody Mass: 360
Center Of Mass Offset: X: 0 Y: 0.7 Z: 1

Transforms:
-----------

Rotors Transform Top: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Main_01 (Transform)
Rotors Transform Tail: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Back_01 (Transform)

Amounts:
--------

Sensitivity: 500
Throttle Amount: 25
Max Thrust: 5
Rotor speed Modifier: 10

Airspeed:
---------

Airspeed Type: Mph *

* or Kmh depending on your desired choice

Max Airspeed: 160 *

* 160 is max suggested for Mph else say 260 for Kmh for example if such was
  selected

HUD:
----

Heli HUD: PoliceHelicopter03_HUD * 

* This will need to be returned to and to then be selected
once you set the interface text mesh pro hud item up in the later step as
described.

Audio:
------

Audio Source: PoliceHelicopter03 (Audio Source)
Rotor Sound: Helicopter03_Rotor


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 122: Modify Settings for: "Rigidbody (Component)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: While the script will work fine and fill these particular settings by itself

instead. So, in saying such, your specific settings should simply look like such:

Mass: 360

Step 123: Modify Settings for: "Mesh Collider (Component)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

instead. So, in saying such, your specific setting should simply look like such:

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

tweaked further to your likings.

Step 130: Identify: the next "Vehicle Prefab"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Let us first identify and locate the "Vehicle Prefab" we are going to use.

Assets > PolygonHeist > Prefabs > Vehicles

SM_Veh_Helicopter_01


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 131: Add: the next "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_Helicopter_01 => "PoliceHelicopter04"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: 72 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonHeist_Material_04_A

Then move "PoliceHelicopter04" into the empty: "Vehicle" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 132: Add: empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "PoliceHelicopter04" add empty as child named "View"

Set the Transform of "View":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 133: Add: "Camera(s)" in empty "View" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "Heli04 Cockpit Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "Heli04 Cockpit Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 2.058 Z: 2.33 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

* Disable the bool in Inspector as this camera is currently just added as an 
optional example and is not currently used, but you could opt for either or a 
future switch method or what not, hence why such is added as an example of three 
diff views.

In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "Heli04 Belly Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "Heli04 Belly Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0.3 Z: 2 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

* Disable the bool in Inspector as this camera is currently just added as an 
optional example and is not currently used, but you could opt for either or a 
future switch method or what not, hence why such is added as an example of three 
diff views.

In the empty: "View" add "Camera" component named: "Heli04 Rear Camera"

Tag: Untagged

Depth: 0

Set the Transform of "Heli04 Rear Camera":

Position: X: 0 Y: 3.2 Z: -10.4 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

* Keep this camera Active as this is the camera we will use (for now).

Step 136: Modify Settings for: "PoliceHelicopter04Controller (Script)" 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: While the script will work fine and fill most of these settings by itself on 
Awake() as intended say as long as you say set the bare minimum for example rotor 
sound & transforms, hmm, let us just for good measure set all up in inspector 
instead. So, in saying such, your settings should simply look like such:

Script: PoliceHelicopter04Controller

Inputs:
-------

Heli Roll Input: Heli Roll
Heli Pitch Input: Heli Pitch
Heli Yaw Input: Heli Yaw
Min Throttle Key: Left Shift
Max Throttle Key: Left Control

Components:
-----------

Rigidbody: PoliceHelicopter04 (Rigidbody)
Mesh Collider: PoliceHelicopter04 (Mesh Collider)

Rb Adjustments:
---------------

Rigibody Mass: 360
Center Of Mass Offset: X: 0 Y: 0.7 Z: 1

Transforms:
-----------

Rotors Transform Top: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Main_01 (Transform)
Rotors Transform Tail: SM_Veh_Helicopter_Blades_Back_01 (Transform)

Amounts:
--------

Sensitivity: 500
Throttle Amount: 25
Max Thrust: 5
Rotor speed Modifier: 10

Airspeed:
---------

Airspeed Type: Mph *

* or Kmh depending on your desired choice

Max Airspeed: 160 *

* 160 is max suggested for Mph else say 260 for Kmh for example if such was
  selected

HUD:
----

Heli HUD: PoliceHelicopter04_HUD * 

* This will need to be returned to and to then be selected
once you set the interface text mesh pro hud item up in the later step as
described.

Audio:
------

Audio Source: PoliceHelicopter04 (Audio Source)
Rotor Sound: Helicopter04_Rotor

Step 146: Add: the next "Vehicle Prefab" to Scene

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Drag the mentioned "Vehicle Prefab" into the scene & unpack the prefab completely.

Next, rename the vehicle prefabs:

SM_Veh_SwatVan_01 => "SwatVan01"

Next, set the Transform:

Position: X: -15 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Material: PolygonHeist_Material_01_A

Then move "SwatVan01" into the empty: "Vehicle" as child of.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Step 149: Add: empty "WheelMeshes" as child

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SwatVan01" add empty as child named "WheelMeshes"

(delete originals after as they are not needed since we copied them into new
location)

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl

Step 150: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SwatVan01" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Front Left Wheel Center X: 5.215406e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Front Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Front Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Front Right Wheel Center X: 0 Y: 0 Z: -1.192093e-07
Front Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Rear Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Rear Left Wheel Center X: 0 Y: 0  Z: 5.960464e-08
Rear Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Rear Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Rear Right Wheel Center X: -4.470348e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Rear Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation


In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.5120534
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.5120534

Set Front Left Wheel Collider Center: X: 5.215406e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Set Front Right Wheel Collider Center: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: -1.192093e-07
Set Rear Left Wheel Collider Center: X: 0 Y: 0  Z: 5.960464e-08
Set Rear Right Wheel Collider Center: X: -4.470348e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0

We will need to now edit these infos:

-----------------

Front Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl(Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr (Transform)

---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

Rigidbody Mass:
---------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 3000

Step 153:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SwatVan01_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SwatVan01_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]

Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...

  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to your
  likings and needs:

Center: X: 0.1047263 Y: 1.611615 Z: 0.8782283
Size: X: 4.096394 Y: 1.665149 Z: 1.00393

Step 156: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SwatVan01Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SwatVan01Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text output display thus such would make sense to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.

Step 166: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SwatVan02" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Front Left Wheel Center X: 5.215406e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Front Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Front Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Front Right Wheel Center X: 0 Y: 0 Z: -1.192093e-07
Front Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Rear Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Rear Left Wheel Center X: 0 Y: 0  Z: 5.960464e-08
Rear Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Rear Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Rear Right Wheel Center X: -4.470348e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Rear Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation


In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.5120534
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.5120534

Set Front Left Wheel Collider Center: X: 5.215406e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Set Front Right Wheel Collider Center: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: -1.192093e-07
Set Rear Left Wheel Collider Center: X: 0 Y: 0  Z: 5.960464e-08
Set Rear Right Wheel Collider Center: X: -4.470348e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0

Step 167: Add to: Van (SwatVan02Controller.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SwatVan02Controller.cs) to "SwatVan02"

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: Van (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl(Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

Rigidbody Mass:
---------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 3000


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 168: Add to: SwatVan02Camera (SwatVan02Camera.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SwatVan02Camera.cs) to "SwatVan02Camera"


Adjust Settings:

Transforms:
-----------

SwatVan02: SwatVan02 (Transform)

Height: 3.28


You can keep settings as is or tweak them to your likings! *

* ie: (tweak camera height)

Height: 3.16


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 169:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SwatVan02_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SwatVan02_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]

Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...

Step 170: Add to: SwatVan02 (SwatVan02Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SwatVan02Entry.cs) to "SwatVan02"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

SwatVan02: SwatVan02
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SwatVan02_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to your
  likings and needs:

Center: X: 0.1047263 Y: 1.611615 Z: 0.8782283
Size: X: 4.096394 Y: 1.665149 Z: 1.00393


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 171: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SwatVan02Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SwatVan02Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text output display thus such would make sense to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 172: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add UI IMG: "SwatVan02_SpeedoGuage"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SwatVan02_SpeedoGuage"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300


In: "Image"


Source Image: Speedometer-Guage

Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF


Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Step 174: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add TMP TEXT: "SwatVan02_SpeedText"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SwatVan02_SpeedText"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 200
Height: 50

Text Input:
-----------

0 mph


Font Size: 36 *

Vertex Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF

Alignment: Center Middle

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.


Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Step 175: In Vehicle > SwatVan02 attach script: (SwatVan02Speedometer.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Speed Text)

Interface Text Object: SwatVan02_SpeedText


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Note: Lastly, in case you missed this notice previously, we need to disable
the listed objects found below as we do not want these objects to display
prior to awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by
default and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive
item in start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable
this object in the editor.

Game Objects:

SwatVan02Speedometer
SwatVan02_SpeedoGuage
SwatVan02_SpeedoNeedle
SwatVan02_SpeedText

Step 181: Duplicate: empty "WheelMeshes" as "WheelColliders"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SwatVan03" duplicate "WheelMeshes" & rename to "WheelColliders"

Set the Transform of "WheelColliders":

Position: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1


Since you duplicated "WheelMeshes" & renamed to "WheelColliders" there should
be the children already present with matching infos...

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr


Prior to the deletion of contents in WheelColliders if you desired to
determine the wheel radius so as to eventually use with Wheel Colliders well,
you could attach a Sphere Collider and gain Radius from that and then delete
the sphere collider after as such would no longer be necessary but instead to
avoid needing to do such I will provide that info so you do not necessarily
need to do so.

These details are important:


Front Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Front Left Wheel Center X: 5.215406e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Front Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Front Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Front Right Wheel Center X: 0 Y: 0 Z: -1.192093e-07
Front Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Rear Left Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Rear Left Wheel Center X: 0 Y: 0  Z: 5.960464e-08
Rear Left Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

Rear Right Wheel Collider Radius: 0.5120534
Rear Right Wheel Center X: -4.470348e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Rear Right Wheel Collider Position Y: 0.6330076 (0.5120534+0.15) *

* Wheel colliders need +0.15 on the Y to function as intended as per
  documentation


In "WheelColliders" children: * (since all are already present in WheelMeshes
and not needed for Wheel Colliders)

* Delete Mesh Filter
* Delete Mesh Renderer

Add Component "Wheel Collider" to each:

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl
SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr

Set both front "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.5120534
Set both rear  "Wheel Colliders" radius: 0.5120534

Set Front Left Wheel Collider Center: X: 5.215406e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0
Set Front Right Wheel Collider Center: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: -1.192093e-07
Set Rear Left Wheel Collider Center: X: 0 Y: 0  Z: 5.960464e-08
Set Rear Right Wheel Collider Center: X: -4.470348e-08 Y: 0  Z: 0

We will need to now edit these infos:


SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.9400756 Y: 0.6330076 Z: 1.927024
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.9400718 Y: 0.6330076 Z: 1.927024
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl
---------------------------

Position: X: -0.9400756 Y: 0.6330076 Z: -1.71297
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr
---------------------------

Position: X: 0.9400718 Y: 0.6330076 Z: -1.71297
Rotation: X: 0 Y: 0 Z: 0 
Scale:    X: 1 Y: 1 Z: 1

Step 182: Add to: Van (SwatVan03Controller.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SwatVan03Controller.cs) to "SwatVan03"

Adjust the following settings:

Require Components:
-------------------

Rigidbody: Van (Rigidbody)

Wheel Transforms:
-----------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl (Transform)
Front Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr (Transform)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl(Transform)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr (Transform)

WheelColliders:
---------------

Front Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fl (Wheel Collider)
Front Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_fr (Wheel Collider)
Rear Left: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rl (Wheel Collider)
Rear Right: SM_Veh_SwatVan_Wheel_rr (Wheel Collider)

Rigidbody Mass:
---------------

Set Rigibody Mass: 3000


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 183: Add to: SwatVan03Camera (SwatVan03Camera.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SwatVan03Camera.cs) to "SwatVan03Camera"


Adjust Settings:

Transforms:
-----------

SwatVan03: SwatVan03 (Transform)

Height: 3.28


You can keep settings as is or tweak them to your likings! *

* ie: (tweak camera height)

Height: 3.16


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 184:  Create child of "VehiclesEntry" add Text tmp: "SwatVan03_EntryKey"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create as a child of "VehiclesEntry" add TextMeshPro Text: "SwatVan03_EntryKey"

Layer: "UI"


Rect Transform: 
---------------

Set at "Top Center"

Position: X: 0 Y: -50   Z: 0 
Width: 100
Height: 100


Text Input: Drive [E]

Font Size: 36

Alignment: Center & Middle

Face:
-----
Dilate: 0.21

Outline: Yes Thickness: 0.121

Underlay: Yes Softness: 0.522

Note: The face, outline and underlay are merely starting suggestions that you
can tweak further to your desired likings as well as any other related
settings of the likes.

Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Ok, now that this part is done we can start moving to other setup steps...

Step 185: Add to: SwatVan03 (SwatVan03Entry.cs)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


Attach component / script (SwatVan03Entry.cs) to "SwatVan03"

Adjust the following settings:


Game Objects:
-------------

SwatVan03: SwatVan03
Player: Player
InterfaceText Object: SwatVan03_EntryKey


In Box Collider:
----------------

Is Trigger: Yes

Edit Collider: YES!* 

* Edit the collider to be around the vehicle doors makings sure to extend the
  collider a good bit out away from doors so as to allow for a good trigger
  zone. Here is just an example that I suggest you tweak further to your
  likings and needs:

Center: X: 0.1047263 Y: 1.611615 Z: 0.8782283
Size: X: 4.096394 Y: 1.665149 Z: 1.00393


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 186: In "VehiclesSpeed" create empty child: "SwatVan03Speedometer"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In "SwatVan03Speedometer"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300

* something to note on placement: ok, when you add the script later in steps
  you will notice an option in script settings for setting on choice of
  either kph or mph in regards to SpeedText output, ok, with taking that into
  account you can now possibly understand the following note about placement
  of the interface items specific to such, mkay lets say that these setup
  steps suggest setting all on the bottom left and that is because we are
  using mph for the speed text output display thus such would make sense to
  have speedometer and speed text on left bottom, but, ok, say you select kph
  as speed text output, then it just might make sence to set the interface
  items to the bottom right and that is why these suggestions are mentioned.
  The choice is yours on that.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 187: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add UI IMG: "SwatVan03_SpeedoGuage"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SwatVan03_SpeedoGuage"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300


In: "Image"


Source Image: Speedometer-Guage

Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF


Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Step 188: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add IMG: "SwatVan03_SpeedoNeedle"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SwatVan03_SpeedoNeedle"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 300
Height: 300


In: "Image"


Source Image: Speedometer-Needle

Color: (Suggested Hex) 6B3232


Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.

Step 189: In Interface > Canvas > VehiclesSpeed add TMP TEXT: "SwatVan03_SpeedText"

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------


In: "SwatVan03_SpeedText"

Adjust:

Rect Transform:
---------------

Middle Center

Width: 200
Height: 50

Text Input:
-----------

0 mph


Font Size: 36 *

Vertex Color: (Suggested Hex) FFFFFF

Alignment: Center Middle

Face:
Dilate: 0.21 *

Outline: YES
Thickness: 0.121 *

Underlay: YES
Dilate: 0.02 *
Softness: 0.522 *

* Note these are just suggestions for you then to tweak and adjust further to
  your likings.


Note: Lastly, disable this object as we do not want this to display prior to
awake or start methods and to do this we will disable this object by default
and then there is a wrapper in the script that will find the inactive item in
start thus doing what will be needed. So yeah, make sure to disable this
object in the editor.
